Back to [dbc files](dbc_files) list.

### \`SoundEntries\` dbc

This dbc contains all sounds-entries used by the client.

**Version is : 3.3.5a**

### Structure

| **Field Nb** | **Name** | **Type** |
|--------------|----------|----------|
| 1            | ID       | Int      |
| 3            | Name     | String   |

### Content
